Monster Spoilers for UnAngband Version 0.5.3
------------------------------------------

The Filthy street urchin  (Red 't')
=== Num:1  Lev:0  Rar:2  Spd:+0  Hp:1d4  Ac:1  Exp:0
He looks squalid and thoroughly revolting.  This thief lives in the town,
and moves a bit erratically at normal speed.  He can open doors, pick up
objects and hide in unusual places.  He needs light to see you.  He takes
quite a while to see intruders, which he may notice from 40 feet.  He
usually appears in groups.  He can beg to nothing, and touch to steal gold.
 

The Scrawny cat  (L.Umber 'f')
=== Num:2  Lev:0  Rar:3  Spd:+0  Hp:1d2  Ac:1  Exp:0
A skinny little furball with sharp claws and a menacing look.  This animal
lives in the town, and moves a bit erratically at normal speed.  It is
fairly observant of intruders, which it may notice from 300 feet.  It can
claw to attack with damage 1d1.  

The Scruffy little dog  (L.Umber 'C')
=== Num:3  Lev:0  Rar:3  Spd:+0  Hp:1d3  Ac:1  Exp:0
A thin flea-ridden mutt, growling as you get close.  This animal lives in
the town, and moves a bit erratically at normal speed.  It is observant of
intruders, which it may notice from 200 feet.  It can bite to attack with
damage 1d1.  

[U] Farmer Maggot  (L.Slate 'h')
=== Num:4  Lev:0  Rar:4  Spd:+0  Hp:350  Ac:10  Exp:0
He's lost his dogs.  He's had his mushrooms stolen.  He's not a happy
hobbit!  This creature lives in the town, and moves at normal speed.  He
can illuminate the dungeon, open doors and bash down doors.  He cannot be
confused or slept.  He is very observant of intruders, which he may notice
from 400 feet.  He may carry a good object.  He can moan to nothing, and
moan to nothing.  

The Blubbering idiot  (White 't')
=== Num:5  Lev:0  Rar:1  Spd:+0  Hp:1d2  Ac:1  Exp:0
He tends to blubber a lot.  This person lives in the town, and moves a bit
erratically at normal speed.  He can illuminate the dungeon and pick up
objects.  He needs light to see you.  He is ever vigilant for intruders,
which he may notice from 60 feet.  He can drool on you to nothing.

=== Num:6  Lev:0  Rar:1  Spd:+0  Hp:1d2  Ac:1  Exp:0

 He can drool on you to nothing.

The Squint-eyed rogue  (L.Red 't')
=== Num:10  Lev:0  Rar:1  Spd:+0  Hp:2d8  Ac:8  Exp:0
A hardy, street-wise crook that knows an easy catch when it sees one.  This
evil thief lives in the town, and moves at normal speed.  He can open
doors, bash down doors, pick up objects and hide in unusual places.  He
needs light to see you.  He pays very little attention to intruders, which
he may notice from 100 feet.  He may carry a object or treasure.  He can
hit to attack with damage 1d6, touch to steal items, and insult to nothing.

doors, bash down doors and pick up objects.  He needs light to see you.  He
prefers to ignore intruders, which he may notice from 100 feet.  He may
carry a treasure.  He can hit to attack with damage 1d3.

=== Num:617  Lev:0  Rar:4  Spd:+0  Hp:350  Ac:10  Exp:0

people by letting Saruman's thugs into the city.  This person lives in the
town, and moves at normal speed.  He may gaze at you.  He can illuminate

he may notice from 400 feet.  He may carry a good object.  He can gaze to

The Grey mushroom patch  (Slate ',')
=== Num:16  Lev:1  Rar:1  Spd:+0  Hp:1d2  Ac:1  Exp:1

1, and moves at normal speed, but does not deign to chase intruders.  It
may release spores.  It is not detected by telepathy.  It resists poison.
 It cannot be frightened, confused or slept.  It is ever vigilant for
intruders, which it may notice from 20 feet.  It may carry one or two
mushrooms.  It can release spores to confuse with damage 1d4.

He is one of the few true masters of the art, being extremely skillful in
all forms of unarmed combat and controlling the world's natural creatures
with disdainful ease.  This shaman is normally found on dungeon level 57,
and moves very quickly.  He is magical, casting spells which cause mind
blasting, heal-self, summon animals, summon spiders or summon hounds; 1
time in 3.  He can open doors and bash down doors.  He is invisible.  He

He may carry up to 8 objects.  He can kick to attack with damage 20d2, kick
to attack with damage 10d2, hit to poison with damage 20d1, and hit to
paralyze with damage 15d1.

He is Morgoth's most powerful servant.  Mighty in spells and enchantments,
he created the One Ring.  His eyes glow with power and his gaze seeks to
destroy your soul.  He has many servants, and rarely fights without them.
 This evil person is found on dungeon level 99, and moves very quickly.  He
is magical, casting spells intelligently which produce fire balls, produce
nether balls, produce water balls, invoke mana storms, invoke darkness
storms, cause brain smashing, cause mortal wounds, produce mana bolts,
produce plasma bolts, produce ice bolts, terrify, blind, teleport-self,
teleport level, cause amnesia, summon monsters, summon Greater Undead,
summon Ancient Dragons, summon Greater Demons, summon Ring Wraiths or
summon Unique Monsters; 1 time in 2.  He can open doors, bash down doors
and push past weaker monsters.  He regenerates quickly.  He resists
lightning, fire, cold and poison.  He cannot be frightened, confused or
slept.  He is ever vigilant for intruders, which he may notice from 1000
feet.  He may carry up to 18 exceptional objects.  He can hit to disenchant
with damage 10d12, hit to disenchant with damage 10d12, hit to drain
charges with damage 8d12, and hit to drain charges with damage 8d12.  You
feel an intense desire to kill this monster...  

[Q] Morgoth, Lord of Darkness  (L.Dark 'M')
=== Num:547  Lev:100  Rar:1  Spd:+30  Hp:20000  Ac:150  Exp:60000
He is the Master of the Pits of Angband.  His figure is like a black
mountain crowned with lightning.  He rages with everlasting anger, his body
scarred by Fingolfin's eight mighty wounds.  He can never rest from his
pain, but seeks forever to dominate all that is light and good in the
world.  He is the origin of man's fear of darkness and created many foul
creatures with his evil powers.  Orcs, Dragons, and Trolls are his most
foul corruptions, causing much pain and suffering in the world to please
him.  His disgusting visage, twisted with evil, is crowned with iron, the
two remaining Silmarils forever burning him.  Grond, the mighty Hammer of
the Underworld, cries defiance as he strides towards you to crush you to a
pulp!  This evil creature is found on dungeon level 100, and moves
incredibly quickly.  He is magical, casting spells intelligently which
produce nether balls, invoke mana storms, cause brain smashing, produce
mana bolts, summon monsters, summon an angel, summon Greater Undead, summon
Ancient Dragons, summon Greater Demons, summon Ring Wraiths or summon
Unique Monsters; 1 time in 3.  He can bore through walls and push past
weaker monsters.  He regenerates quickly.  He resists acid, lightning,
fire, cold and poison.  He cannot be frightened, confused or slept.  He is
ever vigilant for intruders, which he may notice from 1000 feet.  He may
carry up to 20 exceptional objects.  He can hit to shatter with damage
20d10, hit to shatter with damage 20d10, hit to reduce all stats with
damage 10d12, and touch to drain charges.  You feel an intense desire to
kill this monster...
